<th>Incipit
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
<dl><dd><img src="/images/lilypond/ccf663796385c05322eab30405670882.png" alt="\relative c'' { \time 2/4 \key e \major \tempo &quot;Andante&quot;&#10;    gis'4(_\markup { \dynamic p \italic &quot;dolce&quot; } b,8 gis')&#10;    fis[(_\markup { \italic &quot;legatiss.&quot; } e) dis e(]\&lt;&#10;    a4*1/4)-. s8.\! a4--&#10;    a(\> b,8)\! r&#10;    gis'4( bis,8 gis')&#10;    fis[( e) dis e](\&lt;&#10;    fis4*1/4) s8.\! fis4--&#10;    fis4.(\> fisis8)\! }" />
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>

</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Two vocal versions adapted by <a href="/wiki/Category:Laistner,_Max" title="Category:Laistner, Max">Max  Laistner</a> (1853  1917), were published ca. 1900&#160;: "Pansies" with words by <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Percy_Edward_Pinkerton">Percy Pinkerton</a> 
and "Woo thou, sweet music" with words by A.C. Bunten.
</p>
